Created in setUp so each test can load it.\n  @Before\n  public void createRuleBzlFiles() throws Exception {\n    // Rule with a mandatory string attribute and an optional string attribute with a default.\n    scratch.file(\n        \"rules/my_rule.bzl\",\n        \"\"\"\n        def _impl(ctx):\n          pass\n\n        my_rule = rule(\n          implementation = _impl,\n          attrs = {\n            \"required_str\": attr.string(mandatory = True),\n            \"optional_str\": attr.string(default = \"default_value\"),\n            \"str_list\":     attr.string_list(),\n            \"src_label\":    attr.label(allow_single_file = True),\n            \"src_labels\":   attr.label_list(allow_files = True),\n          },\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    scratch.file(\"rules/BUILD\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Helper methods\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  private Package loadPackage(String pkgid) throws Exception {\n    return getTarget(\"//\" + pkgid + \":BUILD\").getPackage();\n  }\n\n  private static AttributeMap attributes(Rule rule) {\n    return RawAttributeMapper.of(rule);\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: basic rule instantiation with required attributes\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void basicRuleInstantiation_succeeds() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) pkg.getTarget(\"my_target\");\n    assertThat(rule).isNotNull();\n    assertThat(rule.getRuleClass()).isEqualTo(\"my_rule\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: missing required attribute produces an error\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void missingRequiredAttribute_producesError() throws Exception {\n    reporter.removeHandler(failFastHandler);\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(name = \"my_target\")\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isTrue();\n    assertContainsEvent(\"required_str\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: default attribute values are applied when attribute is omitted\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void defaultAttributeValue_isAppliedWhenOmitted() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) pkg.getTarget(\"my_target\");\n    String optVal = attributes(rule).get(\"optional_str\", Type.STRING);\n    assertThat(optVal).isEqualTo(\"default_value\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: explicitly supplied attribute value overrides the default\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void explicitAttributeValue_overridesDefault() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n            optional_str = \"custom\",\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) pkg.getTarget(\"my_target\");\n    String optVal = attributes(rule).get(\"optional_str\", Type.STRING);\n    assertThat(optVal).isEqualTo(\"custom\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: passing a list where a string is expected produces an error\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void wrongTypeForStringAttribute_producesError() throws Exception {\n    reporter.removeHandler(failFastHandler);\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = [\"not\", \"a\", \"string\"],\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isTrue();\n    // The error message should mention the attribute or type mismatch.\n    assertContainsEvent(\"required_str\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: string_list attribute accepts a list of strings\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void stringListAttribute_acceptsListOfStrings() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n            str_list = [\"a\", \"b\", \"c\"],\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) pkg.getTarget(\"my_target\");\n    List<String> strList = attributes(rule).get(\"str_list\", Type.STRING_LIST);\n    assertThat(strList).containsExactly(\"a\", \"b\", \"c\").inOrder();\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: passing a string where a list is expected produces an error\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void wrongTypeForListAttribute_producesError() throws Exception {\n    reporter.removeHandler(failFastHandler);\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n            str_list = \"not_a_list\",\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isTrue();\n    assertContainsEvent(\"str_list\");\n  }\n\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: label attribute accepts a valid label string\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void labelAttribute_acceptsValidLabel() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\"pkg/a.txt\", \"\");\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n            src_label = \"a.txt\",\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  // Test: label_list attribute accepts a list of valid labels\n  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n  @Test\n  public void labelListAttribute_acceptsValidLabels() throws Exception {\n    scratch.file(\"pkg/a.txt\", \"\");\n    scratch.file(\"pkg/b.txt\", \"\");\n    scratch.file(\n        \"pkg/BUILD\",\n        \"\"\"\n        load(\"//rules:my_rule.bzl\", \"my_rule\")\n        my_rule(\n            name = \"my_target\",\n            required_str = \"hello\",\n            src_labels = [\"a.txt\", \"b.txt\"],\n        )\n        \"\"\");\n    Package pkg = loadPackage(\"pkg\");\n\n    assertNoEvents();\n    assertThat(pkg.containsErrors()).isFalse();\n    Rule rule = (Rule) pkg.getTarget(\"my_target\");\n    List<Label> srcLabels = attributes(rule).get(\"src_labels\", BuildType.LABEL_LIST);\n    assertThat(srcLabels)\n        .containsExactly(\n            Label.parseCanonical(\"//pkg:a.txt\"),\n            Label.parseCanonical(\"//pkg:b.txt\"))\n        .inOrder();\n  }\n\n  //
